## Historical Capability Evidence

This section is historical capability evidence. The current active plan and recommended next plan are authoritative only in `engine/agent/manifest.json` and the plan registry. The SDL3 removal milestone and `Reviewed Importers Codecs And Shader Generation v1` are closed in the current branch; at that historical checkpoint the composed manifest selected `recommendedNextPlan.id = native-win32-editor-shell-v1`.

After AI Gameplay Authoring Tools v1 implementation merged through PR #174 / commit `9bffa2b8` and the selection-gate closeout pointer sync merged through PR #175 / commit `f05136e2`, the post-1.0 / 1.x candidate program closed at Phase 2 through PR #178 / commit `f4faf787`. At that closeout, the composed manifest pointed `currentActivePlan` back to the production-completion master plan with `recommendedNextPlan.id = next-production-gap-selection` and `unsupportedProductionGaps = []`; current live pointers are manifest-led and may differ from that historical closeout state. Phase 1 added first-party physics constraints/joints evidence, and Phase 2 added value-only kinematic motion plus public simple vehicle policy/package evidence while broad vehicle dynamics, persistent/full crowd simulation, hierarchical navigation, and large-world/persistence remain post-1.0 selection-pool work. `Generated Game Studio v1` is completed for its narrow AI game-creation orchestration surface. `Engine 1.0 Gap Matrix v1` completed the docs/manifest governance selection pass, the selected `renderer-backend-parity-v1` strict Vulkan follow-up landed package-generated mapping compute SPIR-V proof plus reviewed validation-recipe execution, and `Renderer Production VFX Profiling Host Gate v1` completed selected D3D12 and strict Vulkan host-evidence-backed renderer/VFX/profiling counters while Metal remains Apple-host-gated. `Engine General Production Quality Expansion v1` is now completed for selected renderer quality, runtime UI text/font/IME/accessibility contract evidence, broad reviewed import, physics/navigation breadth, networking security/execution, audio production, and generated 2D/3D package evidence without broad ready claims. `Renderer Production Quality And Backend Parity v1` completed the first child of `Clean Break Broad Production Readiness Master Plan v1` through PR #261, PR #262, and PR #263 while broad renderer quality and Metal parity remain host-gated or unclaimed. `Runtime UI Text Platform Stack v1` completed the second child through PR #264, PR #265, PR #266, PR #267, and PR #268 while broad runtime UI platform parity remains host/dependency-gated or unclaimed. `First-Party Desktop Platform And SDL3 Removal v1` completed the Windows-first clean-break removal of SDL3 source, tests, dependency records, CMake/export/install hooks, active docs, and agent contract references. `Reviewed Importers Codecs And Shader Generation v1` then completed selected KTX2/Basis review, glTF scene import review, source image/audio codec review, and reviewed shader generation/cache rows while `unsupportedProductionGaps = []` remains unchanged.

`2D Packaged Playable Generation Loop v1` completed the generated packaged 2D scaffold contract through `DesktopRuntime2DPackage`, cooked sprite/material/audio/orthographic scene payloads, manifest package files, manifest runtime scene validation targets, and focused static checks.

This is a backend-neutral compute dispatch foundation; generated D3D12 POSITION compute morph package smoke is covered by the later generated 3D package slice, and this foundation alone is not async compute overlap, frame-graph scheduling, Vulkan/Metal compute parity, skin+morph composition, or broad renderer quality.

This is a Vulkan backend compute foundation only; Runtime RHI Compute Morph Vulkan Proof v1 is complete for POSITION readback through `MK_VULKAN_TEST_COMPUTE_MORPH_SPV`; Runtime RHI Compute Morph Renderer Consumption Vulkan v1 is complete through `MK_VULKAN_TEST_COMPUTE_MORPH_RENDER_VERTEX_SPV` / `MK_VULKAN_TEST_COMPUTE_MORPH_RENDER_FRAGMENT_SPV`; Runtime RHI Compute Morph NORMAL/TANGENT Output Vulkan v1 is complete through `MK_VULKAN_TEST_COMPUTE_MORPH_TANGENT_FRAME_SPV`; Generated 3D Compute Morph Package Smoke Vulkan v1 is complete for generated `DesktopRuntime3DPackage` POSITION compute morph package smoke; Generated 3D Compute Morph NORMAL/TANGENT Package Smoke Vulkan v1 is complete through tangent-frame SPIR-V artifacts and `Win32DesktopPresentationVulkanSceneRendererDesc::enable_compute_morph_tangent_frame_output`; Generated 3D Compute Morph Skin Package Smoke Vulkan v1 is complete through skinned SPIR-V artifacts, `Win32DesktopPresentationVulkanSceneRendererDesc::compute_morph_skinned_shader`, explicit `compute_morph_skinned_mesh_bindings`, and package-visible `scene_gpu_compute_morph_skinned_*` counters; async overlap/performance, Metal parity, graphics morph+skin composition, and broad renderer quality remain unsupported.

`Runtime RHI Compute Morph D3D12 Proof v1` adds Runtime RHI Compute Morph D3D12 Proof v1: `MK_runtime_rhi` now exposes `RuntimeMorphMeshComputeBinding` and `mirakana::runtime_rhi::create_runtime_morph_mesh_compute_binding`, which bind a position-only base mesh vertex buffer, morph POSITION delta storage, morph weight uniform data, and a compute-write output POSITION storage buffer through first-party RHI descriptor sets. The D3D12 proof dispatches a compute shader with `IRhiCommandList::dispatch` and reads back deterministic `base + weighted deltas` bytes from the output position buffer. This is a D3D12 primary-lane output-position readback proof only; renderer consumption of the compute output, optional NORMAL/TANGENT compute output, and generated D3D12 compute morph package smokes are covered by later slices, while async compute overlap, Vulkan/Metal parity, skin+morph composition, and broad renderer quality remain follow-up work.

`Runtime RHI Compute Morph Renderer Consumption D3D12 v1` adds Runtime RHI Compute Morph Renderer Consumption D3D12 v1: `MK_runtime_rhi` now exposes `mirakana::runtime_rhi::make_runtime_compute_morph_output_mesh_gpu_binding`, which turns a vertex-usage compute morph output POSITION buffer plus the original runtime mesh index buffer into a renderer `MeshGpuBinding`. The D3D12 proof dispatches compute morph, orders graphics consumption through the later public queue-wait contract, draws the output through `RhiFrameRenderer`, and reads back visible center-pixel color from the compute-morphed triangle. This is a D3D12 primary-lane renderer-consumption proof; generated D3D12 package smokes and direct NORMAL/TANGENT compute output are covered by later slices, while async compute overlap, Vulkan/Metal parity, skin+morph composition, directional-shadow morph rendering, and broad renderer quality remain follow-up work.

`Generated 3D Compute Morph Package Smoke D3D12 v1` adds Generated 3D Compute Morph Package Smoke D3D12 v1: generated `DesktopRuntime3DPackage` scaffolds emit D3D12 `vs_compute_morph` and `cs_compute_morph_position` artifacts, package smoke args include `--require-compute-morph`, `MK_runtime_host_win32_presentation` performs the host-owned compute dispatch through public RHI contracts, and `SceneGpuBindingInjectingRenderer` renders from the compute-written POSITION output while reporting `scene_gpu_compute_morph_mesh_bindings`, `scene_gpu_compute_morph_dispatches`, `scene_gpu_compute_morph_mesh_resolved`, and `scene_gpu_compute_morph_draws`. This is the POSITION-output D3D12 generated package smoke; the later tangent-frame package slice adds optional generated NORMAL/TANGENT compute output, while async compute overlap, Vulkan/Metal parity, skin+morph composition, directional-shadow morph rendering, scene-schema compute-morph authoring, and broad renderer quality remain follow-up work.

`Runtime RHI Compute Morph Normal Tangent Output D3D12 v1` adds Runtime RHI Compute Morph NORMAL/TANGENT Output D3D12 v1: `RuntimeMorphMeshComputeBindingOptions` now has opt-in `output_normal_usage` and `output_tangent_usage`, `RuntimeMorphMeshComputeBinding` carries optional output NORMAL/TANGENT buffers, byte counts, and buffer descriptors, and `create_runtime_morph_mesh_compute_binding` binds morph normal/tangent delta inputs plus compute-write output buffers when those streams are present. D3D12 readback tests dispatch a compute shader that writes normalized morphed NORMAL and TANGENT rows through public RHI descriptors. This is the direct D3D12 primary-lane compute output evidence; the generated package promotion is covered by the later tangent-frame package slice, while async compute overlap, Vulkan/Metal parity, skin+morph composition, directional-shadow morph rendering, scene-schema compute-morph authoring, and broad renderer quality remain follow-up work.

`Generated 3D Compute Morph Normal Tangent Package Smoke D3D12 v1` adds Generated 3D Compute Morph NORMAL/TANGENT Package Smoke D3D12 v1: generated `DesktopRuntime3DPackage` scaffolds can request `--require-compute-morph-normal-tangent`, emit tangent-frame compute VS/CS artifacts, pass explicit NORMAL/TANGENT output usage through the Win32 D3D12 scene renderer descriptor, bind compute-written POSITION/NORMAL/TANGENT vertex streams, and report `scene_gpu_compute_morph_tangent_frame_output`. This is D3D12 generated package smoke only; Vulkan/Metal parity, async compute overlap, skin+morph composition, directional-shadow morph rendering, scene-schema compute-morph authoring, public native handles, and broad renderer quality remain unsupported until separately validated.

`Runtime RHI Compute Morph Queue Synchronization D3D12 v1` adds Runtime RHI Compute Morph Queue Synchronization D3D12 v1: `IRhiDevice::wait_for_queue(QueueKind, FenceValue)` and `RhiStats::queue_waits` / `queue_wait_failures` are now backend-neutral public contracts, NullRHI validates queue waits deterministically, D3D12 routes through private queue/fence primitives, and the compute morph renderer-consumption proof orders graphics queue work on the compute fence without a CPU wait between compute submit and graphics consumption.

`Runtime Scene RHI Compute Morph Skin Palette D3D12 v1` adds Runtime Scene RHI Compute Morph Skin Palette D3D12 v1: `MK_runtime_scene_rhi` accepts `RuntimeSceneComputeMorphSkinnedMeshBinding` rows, builds POSITION-only compute base uploads from cooked skinned payloads, retains `RuntimeMorphMeshComputeBinding` resources, inserts compute-morphed skinned bindings into `SceneSkinnedGpuBindingPalette`, and reports `compute_morph_skinned_mesh_bindings` / `compute_morph_output_position_bytes` without exposing RHI or native handles to gameplay. Runtime RHI Compute Morph Async Overlap Evidence D3D12 v1 completes a runtime/RHI-only `RhiAsyncOverlapReadinessDiagnostics` contract and deterministically reports `not_proven_serial_dependency` for the current same-frame graphics queue wait. Runtime RHI Compute Morph Pipelined Output Ring D3D12 v1 is complete; Runtime RHI Compute Morph Pipelined Scheduling D3D12 v1 is complete and adds `RhiPipelinedComputeGraphicsScheduleEvidence` plus `diagnose_pipelined_compute_graphics_async_overlap_readiness` for previous-slot graphics consumption diagnostics. RHI D3D12 Per-Queue Fence Synchronization v1 is complete and adds `FenceValue::queue`, per-queue D3D12 fence timelines, and queue event ordering telemetry. RHI D3D12 Queue Timestamp Measurement Foundation v1, RHI D3D12 Queue Clock Calibration Foundation v1, RHI D3D12 Calibrated Queue Timing Diagnostics v1, Runtime RHI Compute Morph Calibrated Overlap Diagnostics D3D12 v1, RHI D3D12 Submitted Command Calibrated Timing Scopes v1, Runtime RHI Compute Morph Submitted Overlap Diagnostics D3D12 v1, and RHI Vulkan Compute Dispatch Foundation v1 are complete. Runtime RHI Compute Morph Vulkan Proof v1 is complete for proving `RuntimeMorphMeshComputeBinding` POSITION readback on Vulkan through existing public RHI contracts and `MK_VULKAN_TEST_COMPUTE_MORPH_SPV`; Runtime RHI Compute Morph Renderer Consumption Vulkan v1 is complete for Vulkan renderer consumption of that output buffer through `MK_VULKAN_TEST_COMPUTE_MORPH_RENDER_VERTEX_SPV` / `MK_VULKAN_TEST_COMPUTE_MORPH_RENDER_FRAGMENT_SPV`; Runtime RHI Compute Morph NORMAL/TANGENT Output Vulkan v1 is complete for optional tangent-frame output readback through `MK_VULKAN_TEST_COMPUTE_MORPH_TANGENT_FRAME_SPV`. Graphics morph+skin composition beyond recorded package smoke evidence, generated-package measured async compute overlap/performance claims, Metal compute morph parity, broad production frame graph scheduling beyond selected executor/package evidence, directional-shadow morph rendering, scene-schema compute-morph authoring, public native handles, GPU timestamps in gameplay/runtime-host APIs, broad skeletal animation readiness, and broad renderer quality remain unsupported until separately validated.

`Generated 3D Quaternion Animation Package Smoke v1` adds Generated 3D Quaternion Animation Package Smoke v1: committed and generated `DesktopRuntime3DPackage` package rows now ship deterministic cooked/source `animation_quaternion_clip` fixtures, load them through `mirakana::runtime::runtime_animation_quaternion_clip_payload`, decode them with `mirakana::make_animation_joint_tracks_3d_from_f32_bytes`, and sample a one-joint `AnimationPose3d` through `mirakana::sample_animation_local_pose_3d` with `--require-quaternion-animation` smoke counters. This is package/runtime sampling only; animation graphs, retargeting, skeletal renderer deformation, generated-package 3D local rotation-limit authoring/playback wiring, and renderer/RHI execution remain follow-up work.

`Animation 3D Local Rotation Limits Twist Controls v1` adds host-independent 3D local swing/twist constraints for quaternion poses: `AnimationIkLocalRotationLimit3d` rows validate joint indices, duplicate targets, finite twist axes, swing bounds, and twist ranges; `apply_animation_local_rotation_limits_3d` clamps `AnimationPose3d` local unit quaternions; and the constrained FABRIK 3D pose overload reports when limits prevent matching solved positions. This is not authored IK assets, graph authoring, retargeting, skeletal renderer deformation, runtime scene playback, or renderer/RHI execution.

`Animation Fabrik Integrated Rotation Constraints v1` adds solver-integrated XY FABRIK segment local Z rotation limits: `AnimationFabrikIkXyDesc::local_rotation_limits` carries `AnimationFabrikIkXySegmentRotationLimit` rows, the solver validates bounds/ranges/duplicates, and root-fixed reconstruction keeps returned joint positions, rotations, end-effector error, and `reached` consistent with constrained motion. This does not add pole vectors, full 3D IK orientation, angular wrap normalization, authored animation graph workflows, or broad skeletal animation production readiness.

`Animation Ik Angle Wrap Normalization v1` adds signed-pi local Z delta normalization before planar IK clamps: solver-integrated FABRIK segment limits and FABRIK solution-to-pose local rotation clamps now treat `+pi` / `-pi` boundary crossings as small local angle differences. This does not add pole vectors, full 3D IK orientation, quaternion orientation, animation graph workflows, or broad skeletal animation production readiness.

`Animation Two Bone Ik Pole Vector Xy v1` adds planar two-bone IK branch selection through `AnimationTwoBoneIkXyBendSide` and optional `AnimationTwoBoneIkXyDesc::pole_vector_xy`. Pole vectors are finite local XY guide vectors from the root and must be non-collinear with the target; they only select the analytic two-bone elbow side. This two-bone slice itself does not add full 3D IK orientation, quaternion/twist extraction, IK assets, glTF IK import, animation graph workflows, or broad skeletal animation production readiness.

`Animation Two Bone Ik 3D Orientation v1` adds a host-independent analytic two-bone IK 3D orientation basis: `AnimationTwoBoneIk3dDesc` uses a reachable 3D target plus finite non-collinear pole guide, `solve_animation_two_bone_ik_3d_orientation` returns root/elbow/tip positions, and `AnimationTwoBoneIk3dJointFrame` rows expose orthonormal parent/child frames whose `x_axis` points along each solved bone. That two-bone slice itself does not add quaternion clip sampling/application, 3D skeleton pose application, authored IK assets, glTF IK import, animation graph workflows, or broad skeletal animation production readiness.

`Animation Fabrik 3D Chain Ik v1` adds a host-independent 3D FABRIK chain IK position solver: `AnimationFabrikIk3dDesc` carries finite segment lengths, root/target positions, optional initial joint rows, iteration/tolerance controls, and unreachable clamp policy, while `solve_animation_fabrik_ik_3d_chain` returns root-fixed `Vec3` joint positions, end-effector error, iteration count, `reached`, and `target_was_unreachable`. This does not add quaternion clip sampling/application, 3D skeleton pose application, 3D local rotation limits, pole-vector branch control, authored IK assets, glTF IK import, animation graph workflows, or broad skeletal animation production readiness.

`Animation Quaternion Local Pose Foundation v1` adds the first host-independent quaternion local-pose foundation: `MK_math` exposes `Quat`, unit validation/normalization helpers, quaternion vector rotation, and `Mat4::rotation_quat`, while `MK_animation` exposes `AnimationJointLocalTransform3d`, `AnimationSkeleton3dDesc`, `AnimationPose3d`, `AnimationModelPose3d`, `validate_animation_skeleton_3d_desc`, `validate_animation_pose_3d`, `make_animation_rest_pose_3d`, and `build_animation_model_pose_3d` for unit-quaternion 3D local pose storage and model-pose matrices. This does not add quaternion clip sampling/application, glTF quaternion import, 3D IK local rotation limits/twist controls, skinning palette migration, authored IK assets, animation graph workflows, or broad skeletal animation production readiness.

`Animation Fabrik 3D Pose Application v1` adds deterministic 3D FABRIK pose application through `apply_animation_fabrik_ik_3d_solution_to_pose`: ordered parent-child joint chains, valid `AnimationSkeleton3dDesc` / `AnimationPose3d` inputs, finite solved positions, root position matching, and bone-length matching are validated before local unit-quaternion rotations are written. The helper preserves translations, scales, unrelated joints, and the end-effector local rotation, then verifies `build_animation_model_pose_3d` places chain origins at the solved positions. This does not add quaternion clip sampling/application, glTF quaternion import, 3D IK local rotation limits/twist controls, authored IK assets, animation graph workflows, generated-game animation wiring, renderer/RHI integration, cooked asset formats, or broad skeletal animation production readiness.

`Animation Quaternion Clip Sampling Application v1` adds deterministic quaternion clip sampling/application: `QuatKeyframe` and `QuatAnimationTrack` validate finite sorted non-negative keyframe times plus normalized quaternions, `sample_quat_keyframes` uses shortest-path normalized interpolation with clamped sampling, and `AnimationJointTrack3dDesc` / `validate_animation_joint_tracks_3d` / `sample_animation_local_pose_3d` apply selected translation, quaternion rotation, and positive-scale tracks into `AnimationPose3d` while missing components fall back to rest pose. This does not add glTF quaternion import, cooked quaternion clip byte formats, blend trees/graphs over quaternion tracks, animation graph workflows, 3D IK local rotation limits/twist controls, generated-game animation wiring, renderer/RHI integration, or broad skeletal animation production readiness.

`Animation glTF Quaternion Import v1` adds glTF quaternion node animation import: `MK_tools::import_gltf_node_transform_animation_tracks_3d` imports LINEAR glTF node translation, full unit-quaternion rotation, and positive-scale channels into sorted `GltfNodeTransformAnimationTrack3d` rows with `QuatKeyframe` rotation data suitable for `AnimationJointTrack3dDesc` mapping. It now requires an explicit `AssetImportMeshPresetV1` and bakes translation, quaternion basis, and scale into the project right-handed +Y-up meter convention. It keeps the scalar float-clip / transform-binding importer on its z-axis-only `rotation_z` path for y-up rotations and rejects duplicate channels, unsupported interpolation, invalid counts, non-normalized quaternions, and invalid scales. This does not add cooked quaternion clip byte formats beyond the existing quaternion clip path, blend trees/graphs over quaternion tracks, animation graph workflows, 3D IK local rotation limits/twist controls, renderer/RHI integration, or broad skeletal animation production readiness.

`Cooked Animation Quaternion Clip v1` adds the first-party cooked/runtime quaternion clip path: `GameEngine.AnimationQuaternionClipSource.v1`, `GameEngine.CookedAnimationQuaternionClip.v1`, `AssetKind::animation_quaternion_clip`, `runtime_animation_quaternion_clip_payload`, `AnimationJointTrack3dByteSource`, and `make_animation_joint_tracks_3d_from_f32_bytes` carry selected 3D TRS byte rows into `AnimationPose3d` sampling without runtime glTF parsing. `import_gltf_node_transform_animation_quaternion_clip` bridges LINEAR glTF node TRS 3D rows into that source document, and generated 3D package smoke now consumes deterministic cooked quaternion clips. This does not add animation graphs, retargeting, 3D IK local rotation limits/twist controls, renderer/RHI integration, or broad skeletal animation production readiness.

`Animation Fabrik Pole Vector Xy v1` adds planar multi-segment FABRIK branch selection through optional `AnimationFabrikIkXyDesc::bend_side` and `AnimationFabrikIkXyDesc::pole_vector_xy`. Pole vectors are finite local XY guide vectors from the root and must be non-collinear with the root-to-target axis; they select the mirrored XY chain branch while preserving the existing unguided default behavior. This does not add full 3D IK orientation, quaternion/twist extraction, IK assets, glTF IK import, animation graph workflows, or broad skeletal animation production readiness.

`MK_editor` is restored as an optional Windows-native editor/developer shell through the dependency-free `desktop-editor` lane. The shell keeps Win32, first-party retained UI documents, Direct3D 12, DXGI, descriptor heaps, swapchains, fences, Win32 file-dialog/clipboard/process service adapters, private visible D3D12 viewport/material texture display, private RHI texture-display adapter/compositor evidence, and renderer submission private to `editor/src` targets; `tools/build-editor.ps1` is the supported editor configure/build/test lane and `tools/evaluate-cpp23.ps1 -Editor` covers the C++23 editor preset. The current panel set renders Main Menu, Scene, Inspector, Assets, Console, Viewport, Resources, AI Commands, Profiler, Timeline, Project Settings, and Runtime UI Editor from `MK_editor_core` `EditorDockLayout` / `editor_dock_panel_catalog` data stored on `Workspace`, while `MK_editor_core` also exposes value-only dock command planners for show/hide/activate/move/split/reset with validation, confirmation-gated reset, shell chrome/non-native-panel rejection, empty-stack rejection, cycle/duplicate-tab rejection, plan-before-apply revision rows, clean-break workspace v2 save/load, and AI operation snapshot/catalog/dry-run/apply overloads for reviewed dock layout rows, dock command ids, and rich-text rows. `main_menu` is classified as shell chrome, `runtime_ui_editor` is a visible native shell workspace panel, and `input_rebinding` is kept as a workspace panel outside the current native shell panel set. Smoke counters include `editor_shell_ui=first_party`, `editor_shell_backend=d3d12`, `editor_shell_imgui=0`, `editor_shell_panels=12`, `editor_shell_docking_status=single_window_ready`, `editor_shell_dock_tab_headers=12`, `editor_shell_dock_split_gutters=3`, `editor_shell_dock_active_panels=4`, `editor_shell_dock_focusable_controls=12`, `editor_shell_sdl3=0`, `editor_shell_file_dialog_service=win32`, `editor_shell_clipboard_service=win32`, `editor_shell_reviewed_process_runner=win32`, `editor_shell_viewport_status=d3d12_texture_ready`, `editor_shell_viewport_visible_texture_composites`, `editor_shell_viewport_native_handles_exposed=0`, `editor_shell_material_preview_status=d3d12_texture_ready`, `editor_shell_material_preview_visible_texture_composites`, `editor_shell_material_preview_native_handles_exposed=0`, `editor_shell_renderer_boxes_submitted`, `editor_shell_renderer_text_runs_available`, `editor_runtime_ui_editor_panel_visible=1`, `editor_runtime_ui_editor_hierarchy_rows`, `editor_runtime_ui_editor_inspector_rows`, `editor_runtime_ui_editor_style_rows`, `editor_runtime_ui_editor_preview_rows`, `editor_runtime_ui_editor_external_engine_parity_claim=0`, and `editor_runtime_ui_editor_native_handles_exposed=0`. The native shell now has single-window shell-rendered docking tab/gutter UX, active/focused panel styling, hidden-tab disabled command state, keyboard focus traversal over dock tabs, Console diagnostics, AI Commands status/command/evidence rows, Inspector property rows as read-only rich text, Runtime UI Editor retained hierarchy/inspector/style-token/preview/platform-readiness/clean-room rows with text/font, IME, accessibility, renderer-upload readiness, and external-engine parity/native-handle claims at zero, docking smoke counters, private `native_texture_display_adapter.*` evidence for offscreen frame preparation, descriptor updates, barriers, fences, resize safety, visible-compositor-consumption gating, material-preview host-private frame preparation, and private `native_editor_visible_texture_compositor.*` swapchain presentation; selected D3D12 runtime UI atlas upload execution is covered by runtime package evidence, while Vulkan/Metal runtime UI atlas upload execution, Vulkan/Metal editor texture-display parity, broader material-preview GPU parity, multi-window drag/tear-off docking, help rich text, and editable rich text remain future private native/core phases. SDL3 remains absent, public engine/runtime/game APIs do not expose native handles, and runtime game UI remains on first-party `mirakana_ui` contracts rather than Dear ImGui.

`Engine Entity Scale And Culling v1` Phase 1 adds the host-independent entity scale/culling value contract, Phase 2 extends it with LOD and budget intent rows, and Phase 3 adds selected package evidence: `MK_runtime` exposes `RuntimeEntityScaleCullingRequest`, `RuntimeEntityScaleCullingEntityDesc`, `RuntimeEntityScaleCullingViewDesc`, `RuntimeEntityScaleCullingLodBandDesc`, `RuntimeEntityScaleCullingPlan`, and `plan_runtime_entity_scale_culling` for deterministic stable-id sorted visibility/update-bucket/LOD/draw-intent rows over 2D/3D AABB bounds, layer masks, disabled rows, budget-protected row metadata, projected visible/culled/draw/update counters, and fail-closed diagnostics. `sample_2d_desktop_runtime_package --require-entity-scale-culling` now reports `entity_scale_culling_rows`, visible/culled rows, LOD rows, projected draw/update cost counters, budget-protected rows, clean diagnostics, and budget diagnostic counters. This is not scene mutation, gameplay scheduling execution, renderer/RHI residency, GPU/occlusion culling, native handles, or broad high-object-count performance readiness.

## Explicit Non-Ready Claims

Do not claim these as ready unless a focused plan implements them and validation evidence lands:

- broad package cooking and broad background package streaming beyond the reviewed package background read queue
- broad long-running readiness or default long soak validation
- broad Scene v2 package cooking, dependent asset cooking, importer execution, or runtime/package migration beyond the reviewed Scene v2 bridge
- broad renderer/RHI residency, broad residency budgets, or public native/RHI handles for gameplay
- broad automatic cook or runtime ingestion of authored `GameEngine.MaterialGraph.v1` outside the explicit reviewed `plan_material_graph_package_update` / `apply_material_graph_package_update` and `plan_material_graph_production_authoring` surfaces, **full shader graph IR / editor graph UX**, shader compiler execution, live shader generation, broad production sprite batching readiness, or production renderer quality
- tangent-space material/render integration beyond the cooked tangent-frame schema, broader morph pipelines (scene-schema morph authoring, async compute scheduling, skin+morph composition, directional-shadow morph rendering, and broad backend parity), **arbitrary** GPU skinning backend parity beyond the reviewed D3D12 `sample_desktop_runtime_game` skinned mesh + shadow recipe, broader 3D pole-vector branch control, authored IK assets, root-motion motion warping/backward or implicit-duration accumulation, or broad skeletal animation production readiness
- production text shaping implementation, font loading/rasterization, real font-driven glyph atlas generation, runtime image decoding beyond reviewed adapters, broader atlas/editor/runtime integration beyond the reviewed decoded-image and rasterized-glyph package bridges, broad IME parity, non-Windows runtime UI OS accessibility publication, full UIA/screen-reader parity, or cross-platform accessibility parity beyond the private Windows editor UIA provider and selected Windows runtime UIA provider proof
- full editor productization, hot reload, active-session reload/unload, stable third-party binary ABI, broader dynamic game-module/runtime-host embedding beyond reviewed external runtime-host launch, linked-driver handoff, and explicit editor game-module driver load evidence, package script execution from editor core, validation recipe execution from editor core, automatic nested prefab refresh, full nested prefab propagation, or automatic merge/rebase/resolution UX beyond reviewed redundant/duplicate/missing-node cleanup, unique source-node retarget prefab override rows, explicit prefab variant base refresh, explicit scene prefab instance refresh rows, and explicit nested prefab preservation rows
- general generated 3D production readiness
- Metal ready claims without Apple-host validation

Renderer Commercial Readiness Task 10AN note: final handoff withholds the capable-host workflow command until public repository self-hosted runner review is confirmed.
